021078,003581:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
021079,003582: 
021080,003583:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
021081,003584:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
021082,003585:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
021083,003586:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
021084,003587: 
021085,003588:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021086,003589:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
021087,003590:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
021088,003591:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
021089,003592:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021090,003593:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
021091,003594:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
021092,003595: 
021093,003596: 
021094,003597:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
021095,003598:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
021096,003599:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
021097,003600:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
021098,003601:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
021099,003602: 
021100,003603: 
021101,003604:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
021102,003605:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021103,003606:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
021104,003607:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
021105,003608:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
021106,003609: 
021107,003610: 
021108,003611:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
021109,003612:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
021110,003613:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
021111,003614: 
021112,003615: 
021113,003616:                                                                                                  #  .
021114,003617: 
021115,003618: 
021116,003619:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
021117,003620:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
021118,003621:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
021119,003622:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
021120,003623: 
021121,003624: 
021122,003625:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021123,003626:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
021124,003627:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
021125,003628:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
021126,003629:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
021127,003630:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 477 

021129,003632:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
021130,003633: 
021131,003634:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
021132,003635:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
021133,003636:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
021134,003637:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
021135,003638:    4443           10604                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
021136,003639:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
021137,003640: 
021138,003641:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
021139,003642:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
021140,003643: 
021141,003644: 04,2604                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
021142,003645: 04,2604                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021143,003646: 04,2604           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
021144,003647: 04,2605           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
021145,003648: 04,2606           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
021146,003649: 04,2607           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
021147,003650: 04,2610           30001                           CA       L                                     
021148,003651: 04,2611           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
021149,003652: 04,2612           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
021150,003653: 
021151,003654: 
021152,003655:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
021153,003656:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
021154,003657:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
021155,003658:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
021156,003659:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
021157,003660: 
021158,003661:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
021159,003662:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021160,003663:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
021161,003664:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
021162,003665:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
021163,003666:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
021164,003667:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
021165,003668:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
021166,003669:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
021167,003670:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
021168,003671:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
021169,003672:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
021170,003673:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
021171,003674: 
021172,003675:

021324,003827:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
021325,003828:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
021326,003829:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
021327,003830:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
021328,003831:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
021329,003832:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
